<p dir="auto">BT:</p>
<p dir="auto">Grammarkdown (Grmd)</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="http://github.com/rbuckton/grammarkdown">http://github.com/rbuckton/grammarkdown</a></li>
<li>Plain text syntax for specifying ECMAScript grammar</li>
<li>Support for multiple emitters—MD, HTML, Emu</li>
<li>Example</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">AsyncArrowFunction[In, Yield] ::
<code>async</code> [no LineTerminator here] AsyncArrowBindingIdentifier[?Yield] [no LineTerminator here] <code>=&gt;</code> AsyncConciseBosy[?In] #1</p>
<p dir="auto">MM: Can I use this standalone?</p>
<p dir="auto">BT: Sure, but it's just part of Emu</p>
<p dir="auto">Ecmarkup (Emu)</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Emu-xref for cross-references</li>
<li>Emu-production references</li>
<li>Emu-syntax element supports Grammarkdown</li>
<li>In use by SIMD, Intl 2.0, Async Function and others</li>
<li>Michael Dyck now maintaining es-spec-html, working on high-fidelity emu output</li>
<li>Next steps:</li>
<li>Unclock authoring of new specs and porting of 262</li>
<li>New EMD processing model</li>
<li>Continue improving authoring tools</li>
<li>Emd 3.0</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">AWB: note that the Python program that Jason wrote has evolved</p>
<p dir="auto">Ecmarkdown (Emd)</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Working towards 3.0 release</li>
<li>Hand written parser</li>
<li>Support for parsing entre documents (not just single paragraph/list or fragment)</li>
<li>Support for more Markdown-like syntax</li>
<li>Bullet lists</li>
<li>Backslash escape</li>
<li>Next steps:</li>
<li>Unblock authoring of new specs and porting exsting spec</li>
<li>Syntax for links</li>
<li>Smart quotes</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">6.6 BindingRestElement should allow a BindingPattern ala AssignmentRestElement</h2><a id="user-content-66-bindingrestelement-should-allow-a-bindingpattern-ala-assignmentrestelement" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 6.6 BindingRestElement should allow a BindingPattern ala AssignmentRestElement" href="#66-bindingrestelement-should-allow-a-bindingpattern-ala-assignmentrestelement"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">(Brian Terlson)</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="/tc39/notes/blob/main/meetings/2015-07/binding-rest-element.pdf">slides</a></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">BT: AssignmentRestElement allows destructuring, BindingRestElement throws. Destructure rest on assignment, but not on binding</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Historic accident</li>
<li>Bug filed on error thrown by having an array lutera after a rest</li>
<li><a href="https://bugs.ecmascript.org/show_bug.cgi?id=3361" rel="nofollow">https://bugs.ecmascript.org/show_bug.cgi?id=3361</a></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Possible Avenues</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Keep as is</li>
<li>Remove support for a bunding pattern in a rest element</li>
<li>Align AssignmentPattern with BindingPattern to allow further destructuring of the rest element</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto">BindingRestElement[Yield] :
<code>...</code> BindingIdentifier[?Yield]
<code>...</code> BindingPattern[?Yield]</p>
<p dir="auto">Plus necessary statc and runtime semantics to align with BindingPattern</p>
<p dir="auto">MM: Made and fixed this error in <a href="http://research.google.com/pubs/pub43462.html" rel="nofollow">http://research.google.com/pubs/pub43462.html</a></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Any reason to not do the general orthogonal thing?</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">BT: No</p>
<p dir="auto">BT: Babel already treats the same</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Conclusion/Resolution</h4><a id="user-content-conclusionresolution-9" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Conclusion/Resolution" href="#conclusionresolution-9"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Align AssignmentPattern with BindingPattern to allow further destructuring of the rest element</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">6.7 new &amp; GeneratorFunction</h2><a id="user-content-67-new--generatorfunction" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 6.7 new &amp; GeneratorFunction" href="#67-new--generatorfunction"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">(Brian Terlson)</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="/tc39/notes/blob/main/meetings/2015-07/new-generator-function.pdf">slides</a></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">BT:</p>
<p dir="auto">Current Semantics:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>[[call]] <code>this</code> set normally by caller</li>
<li>[[construct]] <code>this</code> is a dynamic ReferenceError</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Issues:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Potentially confusing</li>
<li>new doesn't do anything useful</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Possible Solution:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>GenerationFunction doesn't implement constructor, so new throws</li>
<li><code>this</code> is not a dynamic ReferenceError, but instead refers to the GeneratorFunction instance (align with current implementations: Babel, V8, SM)</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">AWB: Doesn't act like derived constructor, does have a prototype property that's used to initialize instances</p>
<p dir="auto">BT: No case where a subclass will always throw</p>
<p dir="auto">AWB: Body of function is not run as part of the constructor. The body is not a constructor body in the typical sense</p>
<p dir="auto">BT: Breaks down the <code>this</code> and <code>new</code> behavior, b/c can't use <code>this</code> with <code>new</code></p>
<p dir="auto">AWB: The body isn't run as part of the constructor, it's run as "next"</p>
<p dir="auto">DH: A generator used with new is weird. (giving an example)</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="function * Thing(x) {
  this.x = x
}

Thing.prototype.sayHi = function() {};

let thing = new Thing(&quot;tc&quot;, 39);

thing.x // undefined
thing.y // undefined
thing.next();

thing.x // &quot;tc&quot;
thing.y // undefined
thing.next();

thing.x // &quot;tc&quot;
thing.y // 39"><pre><span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-v">Thing</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-v">Thing</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">prototype</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">sayHi</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">thing</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Thing</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"tc"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">39</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-s1">thing</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c">// undefined</span>
<span class="pl-s1">thing</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">y</span> <span class="pl-c">// undefined</span>
<span class="pl-s1">thing</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">next</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-s1">thing</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c">// "tc"</span>
<span class="pl-s1">thing</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">y</span> <span class="pl-c">// undefined</span>
<span class="pl-s1">thing</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">next</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-s1">thing</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c">// "tc"</span>
<span class="pl-s1">thing</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">y</span> <span class="pl-c">// 39</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">DH: Why would want to pause before fully constructing the object?</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Introduces a non-orthogonality that doesn't pay for itself</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">AWB: Generator method</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="let obj = {
  *foo() {
    yield this;
  }
};

let iter = new obj.foo();"><pre><span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">obj</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">*</span><span class="pl-en">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">yield</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">iter</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-s1">obj</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">RW: Non-generator method would throw a TypeError when <code>new ...</code></p>
<p dir="auto">MM/DH: (discussing special cases)</p>
<p dir="auto">BT: Potential argument for why we should allow <code>this</code> inside generator, observables, where you might initialize this before the first yield (by calling <code>next</code> before handing out your iterator)</p>
<p dir="auto">AWB: this binding is actually set up when the iterator is created</p>
<p dir="auto">MM: A generator method, that does not mention super, has a call behaviour that sets this from it's caller the way that a generator function does</p>
<p dir="auto">AWB: imagine "MyCollection"</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="
class MyCollection {
  constructor() {
    // ...
  }
  * values() {
    let k = 0;
    let length = this.length;
    while (k &lt; length) {
      yield this[k++];
    }
  }
}

let collection = new MyCollection();

let values = collection.values();"><pre><span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">MyCollection</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">constructor</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-en">values</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">k</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">length</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">length</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-k">while</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">k</span> <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">length</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-k">yield</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">k</span><span class="pl-c1">++</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">collection</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">MyCollection</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">values</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">collection</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">values</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="
class MyCollection {
  constructor() {
  //
  }
}

let collection = new MyCollection();

collection.values = function * () {
  console.log(this);
};"><pre><span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">MyCollection</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">constructor</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">//</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">collection</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">MyCollection</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-s1">collection</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">values</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">DH: Have a construct trap, normal new object passed in. Generator function is a generator implementation of a function.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>On us to prove/disprove value</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">BN: If trying to discourage using new, this may already be the case, since this.next(), this.throw(), this.return() will all throw if called from within the generator, because the generator is already executing</p>
<p dir="auto">AWB: Cannot re-enter</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="function * Thing(x, y) {
  this.x = x  // current ES6: throw here.
  yield;
  this.y = y;
}

Thing.prototype.sayHi = function() {};

let thing = new Thing(&quot;tc&quot;, 39);

thing.x // undefined
thing.y // undefined
thing.next(); // current ES6: ReferenceError on `this`

thing.x // &quot;tc&quot;
thing.y // undefined
thing.next();

thing.x // &quot;tc&quot;
thing.y // 39"><pre><span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-v">Thing</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span>  <span class="pl-c">// current ES6: throw here.</span>
  <span class="pl-k">yield</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-v">Thing</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">prototype</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">sayHi</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">thing</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Thing</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"tc"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">39</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-s1">thing</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c">// undefined</span>
<span class="pl-s1">thing</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">y</span> <span class="pl-c">// undefined</span>
<span class="pl-s1">thing</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">next</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// current ES6: ReferenceError on `this`</span>

<span class="pl-s1">thing</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c">// "tc"</span>
<span class="pl-s1">thing</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">y</span> <span class="pl-c">// undefined</span>
<span class="pl-s1">thing</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">next</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-s1">thing</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c">// "tc"</span>
<span class="pl-s1">thing</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">y</span> <span class="pl-c">// 39</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">(Note that SpiderMonkey doesn't throw at either of the places called out above)</p>
<p dir="auto">DH: The * is a way of saying that you're providing a way to the precise thing you would do by hand, but without the long form hand written</p>
<p dir="auto">RW: Then generator method should throw TypeError when called with new</p>
<p dir="auto">DH: Agreed</p>
<p dir="auto">MM: What is the instance created from whehn a generator method is called with new?</p>
<p dir="auto">AWB: instance of Generator</p>
<p dir="auto">MM:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="let coll = {*values() {}};
let it = coll.values();
it instanceof coll.values; // true"><pre><span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">coll</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">*</span><span class="pl-en">values</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">it</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">coll</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">values</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-s1">it</span> <span class="pl-k">instanceof</span> <span class="pl-s1">coll</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">values</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// true</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">MM: Unseen: allocatiing a new generator instance. Contains an implicit <code>new</code> and implcit constructor body.</p>
<p dir="auto">DH: * imputes an implicit <code>new</code> (in both the method and constructor)</p>
<p dir="auto">MM: Acting like a function that's calling an implicit constructor</p>
<p dir="auto">BT: it's a factory</p>
<p dir="auto">DH: Simpler: "* is never new-able"</p>
<p dir="auto">Alternative 2: a function * has</p>
<p dir="auto">MM:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="let coll = { *values() { this; } }
coll.values(); // ?

coll.items = function * () { this; };
coll.items(); // ?"><pre><span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">coll</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span><span class="pl-en">values</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-s1">coll</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">values</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// ?</span>

<span class="pl-s1">coll</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">items</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-s1">coll</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">items</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// ?</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">DH:</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>S</th>
<th>I</th>
<th>Code</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>?</td>
<td>X</td>
<td><code>{ *foo() {} }</code> (no [[construct]])</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>X</td>
<td>X</td>
<td><code>function * () {}</code> (no [[construct]])</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>?</td>
<td>?</td>
<td><code>function * () { this }</code> is exactly like <code>function() { this }</code></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<p dir="auto">AK (offline): Further spec reading suggests that GeneratorMethods need to have their [[Construct]] removed just like GeneratorFunctions (they both pass "generator" to FunctionInitialize, which is where the decision to set up [[Construct]] is made).</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Conclusion/Resolution</h4><a id="user-content-conclusionresolution-10" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Conclusion/Resolution" href="#conclusionresolution-10"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Maintain spec that cannot construct generator methods (or change spec to make them non-constructible, see above)</li>
<li>Spec change: generator function do not have a [[construct]] trap, so <code>new</code> throws</li>
<li>Call a generator, <code>this</code> should be set by the caller, as is normal (global or undefined)</li>
<li>File Errata</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">6.12 String.prototype.split, its limit argument, and ToLength vs ToUint32</h2><a id="user-content-612-stringprototypesplit-its-limit-argument-and-tolength-vs-touint32" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 6.12 String.prototype.split, its limit argument, and ToLength vs ToUint32" href="#612-stringprototypesplit-its-limit-argument-and-tolength-vs-touint32"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">(Adam Klein)</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://gist.github.com/ajklein/335e0f948c500a0c25dc">https://gist.github.com/ajklein/335e0f948c500a0c25dc</a></p>
<p dir="auto">AK: Issues:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>ES5 (15.5.4.14.5): If limit is undefined, let lim = 2**32-1; else let lim = ToUint32(limit).</li>
<li>ES6 (21.1.3.17.8): If limit is undefined, let lim = 2**53-1; else let lim = ToLength(limit).</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Problems:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Return value is an Array, so a limit greater than 2**32-1 would result in a "malformed" array (one with elements past the end of the array). Iteration over the return value will skip all such elements.</li>
<li>Behavior changes for negative limit: ToUint32 transforms -1 to 232-1; ToLength instead transforms -1 to 0.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">AWB: One of the discussions was to change arrays to be larger</p>
<p dir="auto">AK: That would make sense</p>
<p dir="auto">Discussion about changes</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>break web?</li>
<li>but this will never likely be hit by any real world code</li>
<li>clamping is valued</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Proposal: Revert this spec change. Existing implementations still match ES5, and the old behavior still makes sense (even with ES6's longer String length limit).</p>
<p dir="auto">WH: The spec needs a geocities-style "Under Construction" animated GIF here ;). This was the first phase of a series of changes attempting to move the spec to eliminate the 2^32 array length limit, with the changes spread over time.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Conclusion/Resolution</h4><a id="user-content-conclusionresolution-11" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Conclusion/Resolution" href="#conclusionresolution-11"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Revert this spec change. Existing implementations still match ES5, and the old behavior still makes sense (even with ES6's longer String length limit).</li>
<li>Filed <a href="https://bugs.ecmascript.org/show_bug.cgi?id=4432" rel="nofollow">https://bugs.ecmascript.org/show_bug.cgi?id=4432</a></li>
</ul>
</article></div><div class="d-none"></div></section></div></div></div> </div> <!-- --> </div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="ScrollMarksContainer-module__scrollMarksContainer__Eu7uU" id="find-result-marks-container"></div><div class="d-none"></div><div class="d-none"></div></div> <!-- --> <!-- --> <script type="application/json" id="__PRIMER_DATA__R_1___">{"resolvedServerColorMode":"day"}</script></div>
</react-app>




  </div>

</turbo-frame>

    </main>
  </div>

  </div>
